}
};
}
}

function fetchModules(){
var element = $("#getMoreRecords");
if(element.length === 0){
return;
}
var outerDivTop = $("#gsearchparentdiv").scrollTop();
var outerDivBottom = outerDivTop + $("#gsearchparentdiv").height();//"#gsearchparentdiv"
var elementTop = ( element.offset().top - 200);
if( elementTop &lt;= outerDivBottom ){
Utils.showHideLoadingDiv(true); 
var url = "/crm/GSearch.do?searchword=null"; //No I18N
var params = JSON.parse('{"fromModule"' + ':"' + element.attr("fromModule") + '"}');//NO I18N
params['sModules'] = sModules;
params['searchCategory'] = searchCategory;
params['userOption']="null";
params['nomatchModules'] = nomatchModules;
var selObj=$('#change_menu').find('.sel');
var prm=selObj.data("params"); //No I18N
params["selectedmodule"] = prm ? prm.module : 'Home';//No I18N
//		alert(params.fromModule);
var reqPool =  new crmRequestPool();
reqPool.initiate({
"action"   : url,//No I18N
"data"        : params,//No I18N
"success"       : function(txt){//No I18N
$('#notesForGsearch').remove();
$("#addModules").append(txt);
Utils.showHideLoadingDiv(); 
nomatchModules = $("#nomatchModules").remove().val();
enableRowClick();
fetchModules();
}
});
element.remove();
} 
};

} );
